    WHERE (@__ef_filter__p_0 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR [a].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)) AND (@__ef_filter__p_1 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR ([a].[TenantId] IS NULL))
    ORDER BY [a].[UserName]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a0].[Id], [a0].[CreationTime], [a0].[CreatorUserId], [a0].[RoleId], [a0].[TenantId], [a0].[UserId]
    FROM [AbpUserRoles] AS [a0]
    WHERE @__ef_filter__p_3 = CAST(1 AS bit) OR ([a0].[TenantId] IS NULL)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[UserId]
ORDER BY [t].[UserName], [t].[Id]
